The girl's name Jenna is pronounced JEN-ah. It is of English origin. Fanciful alteration of Jenny with the -a ending; diminutive of Jennifer; variant of Jean (Hebrew) \"the Lord is gracious.\" The name is made famous by a character on the TV series \"Dallas.\" Jenna is also used for blends and compound names. See also Genna. First Daughter Jenna Bush; actress Jenna Elfman.
